msg:The hotel is not easy to travel to. You have to take the bus or call DD.   

About 10-15 yuan 

The hotel has little space. When entering the accommodation, you have to switch the elevator, going up and then going down. 

The air conditioned room is not cool. I will lose the day I stay. The water is not clean. It's like it hasn't been washed. But the bedding is comfortable, but with a broken air conditioner. Makes you feel all bad 

Overall, if compared to hotels priced at 200-300 yuan, general Chinese brands are better.
